et_pb_fullwidth_section et_section_regular lazyloaded"> <section class="et_pb_module et_pb_fullwidth_header et_pb_fullwidth_header_0 et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_dark"> <div class="et_pb_fullwidth_header_container center"> <div class="header-content-container center"> <div class="header-content"> <h1 class="et_pb_module_header">The Leading XR</h1> <span class="et_pb_fullwidth_header_subhead">Medical Anatomy Platform</span> <div class="et_pb_header_content_wrapper"></div> <a class="et_pb_button et_pb_more_button et_pb_button_one" href="https://www.3dorganon.com/contact-us-demo/">REQUEST DEMO </a><a class="et_pb_button et_pb_more_button et_pb_button_two" href="https://store.3dorganon.com/">BUY NOW</a> </div> </div> </div> <div class="et_pb_fullwidth_header_overlay"></div> <div class="et_pb_fullwidth_header_scroll"></div> </section> </div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_1 et_pb_with_background et_section_regular"> <div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_0"> <div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_0  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child"> <div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_0  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light"> <div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p style="text-align:justify;"><strong>3D Organon</strong> is a medical &amp; healthcare education platform for teaching and learning anatomy across virtual reality, desktop, tablet, and mobile devices. 3D Organon VR Anatomy, 3D Organon’s prime solution, is the world’s first fully-featured <strong>VR anatomy software</strong>.</p> <p style="text-align:justify;">With a plethora of life-like anatomy models within immersive environments and an extensive knowledge base of anatomical definitions translated into 16 languages, it transforms the challenging subject of medical anatomy into concrete knowledge readily applied to clinical practice across the world.</p> <p style="text-align:center;"></p></div> class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_1  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light"> <div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>The 2023 edition</h2> <p style="text-align:justify;"><span>The highly anticipated release of&nbsp;</span>3D Organon<span>&nbsp;for 2023 is here</span> and includes over 12.000 anatomical structures across 15 body systems, showcasing new features such as DICOM Viewer, Hand Tracking, VR Web Search, Lounge Area, 3D Organon Medverse, Ultrasound VR Simulator, images, refactored body actions, microscopic models, and a variety of VR environments among others.</p></div> </div> </div> </div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_2 nitro-offscreen"> <div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_3  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough"> <div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_2  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light"> <div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>3D Organon MEDVERSE</h2> <p style="text-align:justify;"><span>The enriched multi-user VR module provides shared anatomy learning experiences where students can interact in the same virtual space. Users can communicate with their tutors and peers in real-time through voice chat and messages, as they magnify structures of interest, and observe and manipulate 3D models from various viewpoints. Our system supports various training scenarios ranging from small learning groups to classroom-size education, where students and teachers can participate in virtual reality.</span></p></div> </div>
